::: {#mwAyA .section mw-section-id="13"}
## Criticisms and controversies {#Criticisms_and_controversies}

::: {#mwAyE .section mw-section-id="14"}
### Cyberbullying and moderation {#Cyberbullying_and_moderation}

Discord has had problems with hostile behavior and
[abuse](//en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cyberbullying "Cyberbullying"){#mwAyM
rel="mw:WikiLink"} within chats, with some communities of chat servers
being \"raided\" (a large number of users joining a server) by other
communities. This includes flooding chats with controversial topics
related to race, religion, politics, and pornography.^[[[\[]{#mwAyY
.cite-bracket}111[\]]{#mwAyc .cite-bracket}]{#mwAyU
.mw-reflink-text}](//en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Discord#cite_note-113){#mwAyQ
style="counter-reset: mw-Ref 111;"}^ In 2017, Discord stated that it has
plans to implement changes that would \"rid the platform of the
issue\".^[[[\[]{#mwAyo .cite-bracket}112[\]]{#mwAys
.cite-bracket}]{#mwAyk
.mw-reflink-text}](//en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Discord#cite_note-114){#mwAyg
style="counter-reset: mw-Ref 112;"}^

Discord has a Trust and Safety department, where they respond to user
reports.^[[[\[]{#mwAy8 .cite-bracket}59[\]]{#mwAzA
.cite-bracket}]{#mwAy4
.mw-reflink-text}](//en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Discord#cite_note-glixel_2017-61){#mwAy0
style="counter-reset: mw-Ref 59;"}[[[\[]{#mwAzM
.cite-bracket}105[\]]{#mwAzQ .cite-bracket}]{#mwAzI
.mw-reflink-text}](//en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Discord#cite_note-polygon_2017-107){#mwAzE
style="counter-reset: mw-Ref 105;"}^ However, because Discord is
centered around private communities, it is difficult to research on its
effectiveness.^[[[\[]{#mwAzc .cite-bracket}113[\]]{#mwAzg
.cite-bracket}]{#mwAzY
.mw-reflink-text}](//en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Discord#cite_note-:2-115){#mwAzU
style="counter-reset: mw-Ref 113;"}^ A study published in [New Media &
Society](//en.wikipedia.org/wiki/New_Media_&_Society "New Media & Society"){#mwAzk
rel="mw:WikiLink"} criticized Discord\'s offloading of server search
functions to unmoderated third-party apps, saying that it facilitates
hateful communities to find new audience.^[[[\[]{#mwAzw
.cite-bracket}113[\]]{#mwAz0 .cite-bracket}]{#mwAzs
.mw-reflink-text}](//en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Discord#cite_note-:2-115){#mwAzo
style="counter-reset: mw-Ref 113;"}^

In January 2018, *[The Daily
Beast](//en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Daily_Beast "The Daily Beast"){#mwA0A
rel="mw:WikiLink"}* reported that it found several Discord servers that
were specifically engaged in distributing [revenge
porn](//en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Revenge_porn "Revenge porn"){#mwA0E
rel="mw:WikiLink"} and facilitating real-world harassment of the victims
of these images and videos. Such actions are against Discord\'s terms of
service and Discord shut down servers and banned users identified from
these servers.^[[[\[]{#mwA0Q .cite-bracket}114[\]]{#mwA0U
.cite-bracket}]{#mwA0M
.mw-reflink-text}](//en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Discord#cite_note-116){#mwA0I
style="counter-reset: mw-Ref 114;"}^
:::

::: {#mwA0Y .section mw-section-id="15"}
### Data privacy {#Data_privacy}

In September 2024, the [Federal Trade
Commission](//en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Federal_Trade_Commission "Federal Trade Commission"){#mwA0g
rel="mw:WikiLink"} released a report summarizing 9 company responses
(including from Discord) to orders made by the agency pursuant to
Section 6(b) of the [Federal Trade Commission Act of
1914](//en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Federal_Trade_Commission_Act_of_1914 "Federal Trade Commission Act of 1914"){#mwA0k
rel="mw:WikiLink"} to provide information about user and non-user data
collection (including of children and teenagers) and data use by the
companies that found that the companies\' user and non-user data
practices put individuals vulnerable to [identity
theft](//en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Identity_theft "Identity theft"){#mwA0o
rel="mw:WikiLink"},
[stalking](//en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Stalking "Stalking"){#mwA0s
rel="mw:WikiLink"}, unlawful discrimination, emotional distress and
[mental health
issues](//en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Digital_media_use_and_mental_health "Digital media use and mental health"){#mwA0w
rel="mw:WikiLink"}, social stigma, and reputational harm.^[[[\[]{#mwA08
.cite-bracket}115[\]]{#mwA1A .cite-bracket}]{#mwA04
.mw-reflink-text}](//en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Discord#cite_note-117){#mwA00
style="counter-reset: mw-Ref 115;"}[[[\[]{#mwA1M
.cite-bracket}116[\]]{#mwA1Q .cite-bracket}]{#mwA1I
.mw-reflink-text}](//en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Discord#cite_note-118){#mwA1E
style="counter-reset: mw-Ref 116;"}[[[\[]{#mwA1c
.cite-bracket}117[\]]{#mwA1g .cite-bracket}]{#mwA1Y
.mw-reflink-text}](//en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Discord#cite_note-119){#mwA1U
style="counter-reset: mw-Ref 117;"}^
:::

::: {#mwA1k .section mw-section-id="16"}
### Use by extremist users and groups {#Use_by_extremist_users_and_groups}

Discord gained popularity with the
[alt-right](//en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Alt-right "Alt-right"){#mwA1s
rel="mw:WikiLink"} due to the pseudonymity and privacy offered by
Discord\'s service. Analyst Keegan Hankes from the [Southern Poverty Law
Center](//en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Southern_Poverty_Law_Center "Southern Poverty Law Center"){#mwA1w
rel="mw:WikiLink"} stated:

> It\'s pretty unavoidable to be a leader in this \[alt-right\] movement
> without participating in Discord.^[[[\[]{#mwA2E
> .cite-bracket}118[\]]{#mwA2I .cite-bracket}]{#mwA2A
> .mw-reflink-text}](//en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Discord#cite_note-NYT-120){#mwA18
> style="counter-reset: mw-Ref 118;"}[[[\[]{#mwA2U
> .cite-bracket}119[\]]{#mwA2Y .cite-bracket}]{#mwA2Q
> .mw-reflink-text}](//en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Discord#cite_note-NYTpodcast-121){#mwA2M
> style="counter-reset: mw-Ref 119;"}^

Citron stated that servers found to be engaged in illegal activities or
violations of the terms of service would be shut down, but would not
disclose any examples.^[[[\[]{#mwA2o .cite-bracket}120[\]]{#mwA2s
.cite-bracket}]{#mwA2k
.mw-reflink-text}](//en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Discord#cite_note-122){#mwA2g
style="counter-reset: mw-Ref 120;"}^

Following the violent events that occurred during the [Unite the Right
rally](//en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Unite_the_Right_rally "Unite the Right rally"){#mwA20
rel="mw:WikiLink"} in [Charlottesville,
Virginia](//en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Charlottesville,_Virginia "Charlottesville, Virginia"){#mwA24
rel="mw:WikiLink"}, on August 12, 2017, it was found that Discord had
been used to plan and organize the white nationalist rally. This
included participation by [Richard
Spencer](//en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Richard_B._Spencer "Richard B. Spencer"){#mwA28
rel="mw:WikiLink"} and [Andrew
Anglin](//en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Andrew_Anglin "Andrew Anglin"){#mwA3A
rel="mw:WikiLink"}, high-level figures in the movement.^[[[\[]{#mwA3M
.cite-bracket}118[\]]{#mwA3Q .cite-bracket}]{#mwA3I
.mw-reflink-text}](//en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Discord#cite_note-NYT-120){#mwA3E
style="counter-reset: mw-Ref 118;"}^ Discord responded by closing
servers that supported the alt-right and far-right, and banning users
who had participated.^[[[\[]{#mwA3c .cite-bracket}121[\]]{#mwA3g
.cite-bracket}]{#mwA3Y
.mw-reflink-text}](//en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Discord#cite_note-Verge-123){#mwA3U
style="counter-reset: mw-Ref 121;"}^ Discord\'s executives condemned
\"white supremacy\" and \"neo-Nazism\", and said that these groups \"are
not welcome on Discord\".^[[[\[]{#mwA3s .cite-bracket}118[\]]{#mwA3w
.cite-bracket}]{#mwA3o
.mw-reflink-text}](//en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Discord#cite_note-NYT-120){#mwA3k
style="counter-reset: mw-Ref 118;"}^ Discord has worked with the
Southern Poverty Law Center to identify hateful groups using Discord and
ban those groups from the service.^[[[\[]{#mwA38
.cite-bracket}122[\]]{#mwA4A .cite-bracket}]{#mwA34
.mw-reflink-text}](//en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Discord#cite_note-124){#mwA30
style="counter-reset: mw-Ref 122;"}^ Since then, several neo-Nazi and
alt-right servers have been shut down by Discord, including those
operated by neo-Nazi terrorist group [Atomwaffen
Division](//en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Atomwaffen_Division "Atomwaffen Division"){#mwA4E
rel="mw:WikiLink"}, [Nordic Resistance
Movement](//en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Nordic_Resistance_Movement "Nordic Resistance Movement"){#mwA4I
rel="mw:WikiLink"}, [Iron
March](//en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Iron_March "Iron March"){#mwA4M
rel="mw:WikiLink"}, and European Domas.^[[[\[]{#mwA4Y
.cite-bracket}123[\]]{#mwA4c .cite-bracket}]{#mwA4U
.mw-reflink-text}](//en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Discord#cite_note-125){#mwA4Q
style="counter-reset: mw-Ref 123;"}^

In March 2019, the media collective [Unicorn
Riot](//en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Unicorn_Riot "Unicorn Riot"){#mwA4k
rel="mw:WikiLink"} published the contents of a Discord server used by
several members of the white nationalist group [Identity
Evropa](//en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Identity_Evropa "Identity Evropa"){#mwA4o
rel="mw:WikiLink"} who were also members of the [United States Armed
Forces](//en.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_States_Armed_Forces "United States Armed Forces"){#mwA4s
rel="mw:WikiLink"}.^[[[\[]{#mwA44 .cite-bracket}124[\]]{#mwA48
.cite-bracket}]{#mwA40
.mw-reflink-text}](//en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Discord#cite_note-126){#mwA4w
style="counter-reset: mw-Ref 124;"}^ Unicorn Riot has since published
member lists and contents of several dozen servers connected to
alt-right, white supremacist, and other such movements.

In January 2021, two days after the [U.S. Capitol
attack](//en.wikipedia.org/wiki/2021_United_States_Capitol_attack "2021 United States Capitol attack"){#mwA5E
.mw-redirect rel="mw:WikiLink"}, Discord deleted the pro-[Donald
Trump](//en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Donald_Trump "Donald Trump"){#mwA5I
rel="mw:WikiLink"} server The Donald, \"due to its overt connection to
an online forum used to incite violence, plan an armed insurrection in
the United States, and spread [harmful
misinformation](//en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Attempts_to_overturn_the_2020_United_States_presidential_election "Attempts to overturn the 2020 United States presidential election"){#mwA5M
rel="mw:WikiLink"} related to [2020 U.S.
election](//en.wikipedia.org/wiki/2020_United_States_presidential_election "2020 United States presidential election"){#mwA5Q
rel="mw:WikiLink"} fraud\", while stating that there was no evidence the
server was used to organize the attack on the [Capitol
building](//en.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_States_Capitol "United States Capitol"){#mwA5U
rel="mw:WikiLink"}. The server had been used by former members of the
[r/The_Donald](//en.wikipedia.org/wiki/R/The_Donald "R/The Donald"){#mwA5Y
rel="mw:WikiLink"}
[subreddit](//en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Subreddit "Subreddit"){#mwA5c
.mw-redirect rel="mw:WikiLink"}, which
[Reddit](//en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Reddit "Reddit"){#mwA5g
rel="mw:WikiLink"} had deleted several months previous.^[[[\[]{#mwA5s
.cite-bracket}125[\]]{#mwA5w .cite-bracket}]{#mwA5o
.mw-reflink-text}](//en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Discord#cite_note-127){#mwA5k
style="counter-reset: mw-Ref 125;"}^

In January 2022, the British
anti-[disinformation](//en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Disinformation "Disinformation"){#mwA54
rel="mw:WikiLink"} organization
[Logically](//en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Logically_(company) "Logically (company)"){#mwA58
rel="mw:WikiLink"} reported that [Holocaust
denial](//en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Holocaust_denial "Holocaust denial"){#mwA6A
rel="mw:WikiLink"},
[neo-Nazism](//en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Neo-Nazism "Neo-Nazism"){#mwA6E
rel="mw:WikiLink"} and other forms of [hate
speech](//en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hate_speech "Hate speech"){#mwA6I
rel="mw:WikiLink"} were flourishing on the Discord and
[Telegram](//en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Telegram_(software) "Telegram (software)"){#mwA6M
rel="mw:WikiLink"} groups of the German website
[Disclose.tv](//en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Disclose.tv "Disclose.tv"){#mwA6Q
rel="mw:WikiLink"}.^[[[\[]{#mwA6c .cite-bracket}126[\]]{#mwA6g
.cite-bracket}]{#mwA6Y
.mw-reflink-text}](//en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Discord#cite_note-:02-128){#mwA6U
style="counter-reset: mw-Ref 126;"}[[[\[]{#mwA6s
.cite-bracket}127[\]]{#mwA6w .cite-bracket}]{#mwA6o
.mw-reflink-text}](//en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Discord#cite_note-:13-129){#mwA6k
style="counter-reset: mw-Ref 127;"}^

In May 2022, Payton S. Gendron was named as the suspect in [a
race-driven mass
shooting](//en.wikipedia.org/wiki/2022_Buffalo_shooting "2022 Buffalo shooting"){#mwA64
rel="mw:WikiLink"} in [Buffalo, New
York](//en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Buffalo,_New_York "Buffalo, New York"){#mwA68
rel="mw:WikiLink"}, that killed ten people. It was reported that Gendron
used a private Discord server as a diary for weeks as he prepared for
the attack. Approximately 30 minutes before the shooting, several users
were invited by Gendron to view the server and read the messages. The
messages were later published on
[4chan](//en.wikipedia.org/wiki/4chan "4chan"){#mwA7A
rel="mw:WikiLink"}. Discord told the press that the server was deleted
by moderators shortly after the shooting.^[[[\[]{#mwA7M
.cite-bracket}128[\]]{#mwA7Q .cite-bracket}]{#mwA7I
.mw-reflink-text}](//en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Discord#cite_note-130){#mwA7E
style="counter-reset: mw-Ref 128;"}^ The New York state attorney
general\'s office announced an investigation of Discord among other
online services in the wake of the shooting to determine if they had
taken enough steps to prevent such content from being broadcast on their
services, with which Discord said they would comply.^[[[\[]{#mwA7c
.cite-bracket}129[\]]{#mwA7g .cite-bracket}]{#mwA7Y
.mw-reflink-text}](//en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Discord#cite_note-131){#mwA7U
style="counter-reset: mw-Ref 129;"}^
:::

::: {#mwA7k .section mw-section-id="17"}
### Child grooming and safety {#Child_grooming_and_safety}

CNN has reported that Discord has had problems with [sexual exploitation
of children and young
teenagers](//en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Child_sexual_abuse "Child sexual abuse"){#mwA7s
rel="mw:WikiLink"} on its platform.^[[[\[]{#mwA74
.cite-bracket}12[\]]{#mwA78 .cite-bracket}]{#mwA70
.mw-reflink-text}](//en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Discord#cite_note-:6-14){#mwA7w
style="counter-reset: mw-Ref 12;"}^

In July 2018, Discord updated its terms of service to ban [drawn
pornography](//en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cartoon_pornography "Cartoon pornography"){#mwA8E
rel="mw:WikiLink"} with underage subjects.^[[[\[]{#mwA8Q
.cite-bracket}130[\]]{#mwA8U .cite-bracket}]{#mwA8M
.mw-reflink-text}](//en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Discord#cite_note-polygon1-132){#mwA8I
style="counter-reset: mw-Ref 130;"}^ Some Discord users subsequently
criticized the moderation staff for selectively allowing \"cub\"
content, or underage pornographic
[furry](//en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Furry_fandom "Furry fandom"){#mwA8Y
rel="mw:WikiLink"} artwork, under the same guidelines. The staff held
that \"cub porn\" was separate from
[lolicon](//en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lolicon "Lolicon"){#mwA8c
rel="mw:WikiLink"} and
[shotacon](//en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Shotacon "Shotacon"){#mwA8g
rel="mw:WikiLink"}, being \"allowable as long as it is tagged
properly\".^[[[\[]{#mwA8s .cite-bracket}130[\]]{#mwA8w
.cite-bracket}]{#mwA8o
.mw-reflink-text}](//en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Discord#cite_note-polygon1-132){#mwA8k
style="counter-reset: mw-Ref 130;"}^ After numerous complaints from the
community, Discord amended its community guidelines in February 2019 to
include \"non-humanoid animals and mythological creatures as long as
they appear to be underage\" in its list of disallowed categories, in
addition to announcing periodic transparency reports to better
communicate with users.^[[[\[]{#mwA88 .cite-bracket}131[\]]{#mwA9A
.cite-bracket}]{#mwA84
.mw-reflink-text}](//en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Discord#cite_note-133){#mwA80
style="counter-reset: mw-Ref 131;"}^

In June 2023, [NBC
News](//en.wikipedia.org/wiki/NBC_News "NBC News"){#mwA9I
rel="mw:WikiLink"} reported that they had identified 35 cases of adults
being charged with
\"[kidnapping](//en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Child_abduction "Child abduction"){#mwA9M
rel="mw:WikiLink"},
[grooming](//en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Child_grooming "Child grooming"){#mwA9Q
.mw-redirect rel="mw:WikiLink"}, or [sexual
assault](//en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sexual_assault "Sexual assault"){#mwA9U
rel="mw:WikiLink"}\" that allegedly involved the platform. They
additionally discovered 165 cases of prosecution for the sharing of
child sexual exploitation material on the platform.^[[[\[]{#mwA9g
.cite-bracket}132[\]]{#mwA9k .cite-bracket}]{#mwA9c
.mw-reflink-text}](//en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Discord#cite_note-134){#mwA9Y
style="counter-reset: mw-Ref 132;"}^

In March 2024, a joint investigation by [The Washington
Post](//en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Washington_Post "The Washington Post"){#mwA9s
rel="mw:WikiLink"},
[Wired](//en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wired_(magazine) "Wired (magazine)"){#mwA9w
rel="mw:WikiLink"}, [Der
Spiegel](//en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Der_Spiegel "Der Spiegel"){#mwA90
rel="mw:WikiLink"} and Recorder outlined the extensive child grooming,
sexual abuse (including
[sextortion](//en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sextortion "Sextortion"){#mwA94
rel="mw:WikiLink"}) and murder conducted by a group known as
*[764](//en.wikipedia.org/wiki/764_(organization) "764 (organization)"){#mwA-A
rel="mw:WikiLink"}* on Discord. The investigation linked 764 and its
associated groups and servers to cases in Germany, United States and
Romania, going as far back as April 2021. Discord\'s representative
stated that the service filed hundreds of reports, in addition to
removing over 34,000 accounts associated with the group.^[[[\[]{#mwA-M
.cite-bracket}133[\]]{#mwA-Q .cite-bracket}]{#mwA-I
.mw-reflink-text}](//en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Discord#cite_note-135){#mwA-E
style="counter-reset: mw-Ref 133;"}[[[\[]{#mwA-c
.cite-bracket}134[\]]{#mwA-g .cite-bracket}]{#mwA-Y
.mw-reflink-text}](//en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Discord#cite_note-136){#mwA-U
style="counter-reset: mw-Ref 134;"}^
:::

::: {#mwA-k .section mw-section-id="18"}
### Bans {#Bans}

On January 27, 2021, Discord banned the
[r/WallStreetBets](//en.wikipedia.org/wiki/R/WallStreetBets "R/WallStreetBets"){#mwA-s
.mw-redirect rel="mw:WikiLink"} server during the [GameStop short
squeeze](//en.wikipedia.org/wiki/GameStop_short_squeeze "GameStop short squeeze"){#mwA-w
rel="mw:WikiLink"}, citing \"hateful and discriminatory content\", which
users found contentious.^[[[\[]{#mwA-8 .cite-bracket}135[\]]{#mwA_A
.cite-bracket}]{#mwA-4
.mw-reflink-text}](//en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Discord#cite_note-137){#mwA-0
style="counter-reset: mw-Ref 135;"}^ One day later, Discord allowed
another server to be created and began assisting with moderation on
it.^[[[\[]{#mwA_M .cite-bracket}136[\]]{#mwA_Q .cite-bracket}]{#mwA_I
.mw-reflink-text}](//en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Discord#cite_note-138){#mwA_E
style="counter-reset: mw-Ref 136;"}^
:::

::: {#mwA_U .section mw-section-id="19"}
### Censorship {#Censorship}

In September 2024, according to Russian media Kommersant, Russian
regulator
[Roskomnadzor](//en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Roskomnadzor "Roskomnadzor"){#mwA_c
rel="mw:WikiLink"} was planning to block the platform.^[[[\[]{#mwA_o
.cite-bracket}137[\]]{#mwA_s .cite-bracket}]{#mwA_k
.mw-reflink-text}](//en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Discord#cite_note-139){#mwA_g
style="counter-reset: mw-Ref 137;"}^ Russian regulator Roskomnadzor
demanded that the platform remove 947 posts containing illegal content
and imposed a 3.5 million roubles (USD\$37,493) fine.^[[[\[]{#mwA_4
.cite-bracket}138[\]]{#mwA_8 .cite-bracket}]{#mwA_0
.mw-reflink-text}](//en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Discord#cite_note-140){#mwA_w
style="counter-reset: mw-Ref 138;"}^ On 8 October 2024, Russia
officially blocked Discord.^[[[\[]{#mwBAI .cite-bracket}139[\]]{#mwBAM
.cite-bracket}]{#mwBAE
.mw-reflink-text}](//en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Discord#cite_note-141){#mwBAA
style="counter-reset: mw-Ref 139;"}^

Following a decision made by the [Ankara 1st Criminal Court of
Peace](//en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Judicial_system_of_Turkey "Judicial system of Turkey"){#mwBAU
rel="mw:WikiLink"}, several hours apart from Russia\'s block, Turkey
blocked Discord.^[[[\[]{#mwBAg .cite-bracket}140[\]]{#mwBAk
.cite-bracket}]{#mwBAc
.mw-reflink-text}](//en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Discord#cite_note-142){#mwBAY
style="counter-reset: mw-Ref 140;"}^

Discord is blocked by the [Great Firewall in
China](//en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Firewall "Great Firewall"){#mwBAs
rel="mw:WikiLink"}. Chinese police will find and interrogate people who
make sensitive comments on the platform.^[[[\[]{#mwBA4
.cite-bracket}141[\]]{#mwBA8 .cite-bracket}]{#mwBA0
.mw-reflink-text}](//en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Discord#cite_note-143){#mwBAw
style="counter-reset: mw-Ref 141;"}^
:::
:::

    Cassandra.\" \"Since Cassandra is eventually consistent it cannot
